            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id

            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id

<h2>What's New in Gravity Forms v1.9.11</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added 'gform_entries_field_header_pre_export', 'gform_entries_field_header_pre_export_{form_id}' and 'gform_entries_field_header_pre_export_{form_id}_{field_id}' filters for modifying the fields header in the entry export.</li>
<li>Added additional accessibility with addition of aria-label to markup.</li>
<li>Updated loading of the text domains to prevent loading them more than once.</li>
<li>Updated list field pre-population to accept an array in the same format currently saved to the database. This change is backwards-compatible and will accept the old array format.</li>
<li>Updated GFFormDisplay::get_input_mask_init_script() to disable the input mask for Android phones. This is a temporary workaround for some issues with certain models of Android phones.</li>
<li>Updated some security hardening precautions.</li>
<li>Updated shortcode parsing so that "form" is the default action.</li>
<li>Updated Finnish translation.</li>
<li>Updated the ajax submission iframe tag to include the title attribute when HTML5 is enabled in the settings to comply with WCAG 2.0.</li>
<li>Removed the duplicate_setting from the multiselect field type.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the select and multi-select type fields which could result in the incorrect choices being selected.</li>
<li>Fixed debug warning notices.</li>
<li>Fixed a formatting issue in the payment results table.</li>
<li>Fixed a warning in debug mode on the updates page.</li>
<li>Fixed fatal error if insert_with_markers() not available.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the updates page not displaying the "No updates available" message appropriately.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with validation of the Reply To field on the edit notification page.</li>
<li>Fixed a minor CSS conflict with the Lite Tooltip plugin.</li>
<li>Fixed issue with number field formatting for certain currencies.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the Swiss Franc currency.</li>
<li>Fixed notices caused by new primary column parameter for classes extending the WP_List_Table class.</li>
</ul>

<h2>Add-On Framework Updates in Gravity Forms v1.9.11</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added 'gform_post_payment_action' hook to allow actions to be taken when payment events are completed. See https://www.gravityhelp.com/documentation/article/gform_post_payment_action/</li>
<li>Added "after_input" property to text field setting to show text after the input field.</li>
<li>Added maybe_override_field_value(). Override to prevent use of the gform_{slug}_field_value filter or to replace with a customised filter.</li>
<li>Added can_create_feed() to control rendering of feed creation UI.</li>
<li>Added "gform_{slug}_field_value", "gform_{slug}_field_value_{$form_id}" and "gform_{slug}_field_value_{$form_id}_{$field_id}" filters to modify field value.</li>
<li>Added "get_first_field_by_type" function to get the field ID of the first field of the desired type.</li>
<li>Updated field map choices to show "Select a Field" as first choice.</li>
<li>Updated field map choices to show message to user asking them to add a field to their form if no fields of designated type were found.</li>
<li>Updated Feed Name to display a default incremented name based on existing feeds in the add-on.</li>
<li>Fixed PHP notice with field select setting field due to undefined first choice label.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the app uninstall confirmation message not displaying.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the feed name in some maybe_process_feed() logging statements.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the default feed name not incrementing correctly based on field name.</li>
<li>Fixed a PHP notice for settings fields if field_type setting property was an array.</li>
<li>Fixed a PHP warning related to sales pagination.</li>
</ul>

<h2>API Updates in Gravity Forms v1.9.11</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue with GFAPI::update_entry_field() where values for field IDs higher than 99 get added instead of updated.</li>
<li>Fixed an issue with the Serbia and Montenegro choices in GF_Field_Address get_countries() and get_country_codes().</li>
</ul>

            FROM wp_rg_lead l

            (

                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.id = 617)
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,1
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            FROM wp_rg_lead l

            (

                (

                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id

            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (

                    WHERE (l.form_id=43 AND l.status = 'active')
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,20
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.id = 622)
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,1
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort
